We’ve enlisted the <strong>world’s top designers</strong> to craft\n      lessons for learning the tools, techniques &amp; terminology of good design.\n    </p>\n  </section>\n\n  <section class=\"interactive large-4 columns\">\n    <h4>Interactive Content</h4>\n    <p>\n      Learn by doing. <strong>Play with design puzzles and challenging games as you learn.</strong>\n      Test your skills and explore possibilities.\n    </p>\n  </section>\n\n  <section class=\"tools large-4 columns\">\n    <h4>Awesome Design Tools</h4>\n    <p>\n      We’ve curated a list of the <a </div>\n        <div class=\"large-12 small-9 columns\">\n          <h5>Kerem Suer</h5>\n          <p>I'm a designer of digital products in my late 20’s who is little too into simplicity and pixel-perfection. I studied interactive visual imaging and photography in Missouri, and somehow ended up in foggy San Francisco designing things with unbelievably talented teams such as <a href=\"https://fitbit.com\" target=\"_blank\">Fitbit</a>, <a href=\"https://pinterest.com\" target=\"_blank\">Pinterest</a>, <a href=\"https://www.zendesk.com\" target=\"_blank\">Zendesk</a>, and <a href=\"https://www.onekingslane.com\" target=\"_blank\">One Kings Lane</a>.</p>\n        </div>\n      </li>\n      <li>\n        <div class=\"large-12 small-3 columns avatar-container\">\n     </div>\n        <div class=\"large-12 small-9 columns\">\n          <h5>Jared Erondu</h5>\n          <p>I'm a writer and designer from Brooklyn, living in Baltimore. I'm the co-founder of <a href=\"http://theindustry.cc\" target=\"_blank\">The Industry</a> (a design publication) and <a href=\"http://evomail.io\" target=\"_blank\">Evomail</a> (an iPad email app). I advise companies <a href=\"http://advise.me\" target=\"_blank\">here</a> and <a href=\"http://6wunderkinder.com/\" target=\"_blank\">there</a>.     </div>\n        <div class=\"large-12 small-9 columns\">\n          <h5>Joanne Chang</h5>\n          <p>I'm a co-founder and design lead at <a href=\"http://pic-collage.com\" target=\"_blank\">PicCollage</a>. It is a fun and easy way to create collages on your mobile devices. I love colors and patterns and the process of bringing ideas to life. and iOS developer. I’m also a designer. I co-host a podcast called <a href=\"http://bjango.com/articles/iterate/\" target=\"_blank\">Iterate</a> with Rene Ritchie and Seth Clifford. Onori</h5>\n          <p>I'm a design technologist living in San Francisco. I have worked for companies such as Adaptive Path, Method and Current TV and worked with clients including the United Nations, Samsung, Adobe, TED.com and Foodspotting.   </div>\n        <div class=\"large-12 small-9 columns\">\n          <h5>Kate Rutter</h5>\n          <p>I'm a maker+designer who loves stickynotes, sketching and startups. At <a href=\"http://luxr.co/\" target=\"_blank\">LUXr</a>, I get to meet incredible entrepreneurs and help them design great customer experiences. I've worked at places like <a href=\"http://adaptivepath.com/\" target=\"_blank\">Adaptive Path</a> and <a href=\"http://thecrucible.org/\" target=\"_blank\">The Crucible</a>.
